Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-103 Use of bond proceeds for issuance and other costs.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be used for the purposes described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-104 Manner of issuance -- Amounts, interest, and maturity.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-104(1): Bonds issued under this chapter may be authorized, sold, and issued at times and in a manner determined by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-104(2): Bonds may be issued in one or more series, in amounts, and shall bear dates, interest rate or rates, including a variable rate, and maturity dates as the commission determines by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-104(3): A bond issued may not mature later than 20 years after the date of final passage of this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105 Terms and conditions of sale -- Plan of financing -- Signatures -- Replacement -- Registration -- Federal rebate.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1): In the issuance of bonds, the commission may determine by resolution:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(a): the manner of sale, including public or private sale;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(b): the terms and conditions of sale, including price, whether at, below, or above face value;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(c): denominations;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(d): form;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(e): manner of execution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(f): manner of authentication;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(g): place and medium of purchase;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(h): redemption terms; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(1)(i): other provisions and details it considers appropriate.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(2): The commission may by resolution adopt a plan of financing, which may include terms and conditions of arrangements entered into by the commission on behalf of the state with financial and other institutions for letters of credit, standby letters of credit, reimbursement agreements, and remarketing, indexing, and tender agent agreements to secure the bonds, including payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under the agreements entered into by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(3)(a): Any signature of a public official authorized by resolution of the commission to sign the bonds may be a facsimile signature of that official imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(3)(b): If all signatures of public officials on the bonds are facsimile signatures, provision shall be made for a manual authenticating signature on the bonds by or on behalf of a designated authentication agent.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(3)(c): If an official ceases to hold office before delivery of the bonds signed by that official, the signature or facsimile signature of the official is nevertheless valid for all purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(3)(d): A facsimile of the state seal may be imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(4)(a): The commission may enact resolutions providing for the replacement of lost, destroyed, or mutilated bonds, or for the exchange of bonds after issuance for bonds of smaller or larger denominations.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(4)(b): Bonds in changed denominations shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(4)(b)(i): be exchanged for the original bonds in like aggregate principal amounts and in a manner that prevents the duplication of interest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(4)(b)(ii): bear interest at the same rate, mature on the same date, and be as nearly as practicable in the form of the original bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(5): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305; Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(5)(a): Bonds may be registered as to both principal and interest or may be in a book entry form under which the right to principal and interest may be transferred only through a book entry.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(5)(b): The commission may provide for the services and payment for the services of one or more financial institutions or other entities or persons, or nominees, within or outside the state, for the authentication, registration, transfer, including record, bookkeeping, or book entry functions, exchange, and payment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(5)(c): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305 The records of ownership, registration, transfer, and exchange of the bonds, and of persons to whom payment with respect to the obligations are made, are private records as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(5)(d): Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act The bonds and any evidences of participation interest in the bonds may be issued, executed, authenticated, registered, transferred, exchanged, and otherwise made to comply with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(6): The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(6)(a): by resolution, provide for payment to the United States of whatever amounts are necessary to comply with Section 148 (f) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(6)(b): enter into agreements with financial and other institutions and attorneys to provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(6)(b)(i): the calculation, holding, and payment of those amounts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-105(6)(b)(ii): payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under any agreements entered into by the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-106 Constitutional debt limitation.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-106(1): The commission may not issue bonds under this chapter in an amount that violates the limitation described in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-106(2): For purposes of applying the debt limitation contained in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1, the value of the taxable property in Utah is considered to be 100% of the fair market value of the taxable property of the state, as computed from the last assessment for state purposes previous to the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107 Tax levy -- Abatement of tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(1): Each year after issuance of the bonds and until all outstanding bonds are retired, there is levied a direct annual tax on all real and personal property within the state subject to state taxation, sufficient to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(1)(a): applicable bond redemption premiums, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(1)(b): interest on the bonds as it becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(1)(c): principal of the bonds as it becomes due.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(2)(a): The State Tax Commission shall fix the rate of the direct annual tax levy each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(2)(b): The tax shall be collected and the proceeds applied as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-107(3): The direct annual tax imposed under this section is abated to the extent money is available from sources, other than ad valorem taxes in the sinking fund, for the payment of bond interest, principal, and redemption premiums.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-108 Creation of sinking fund.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-108(1): There is created a sinking fund, to be administered by the state treasurer, entitled the "1997 General Obligation Bonds Sinking Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-108(2): All money deposited in the sinking fund, from whatever source, shall be used to pay debt service on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-108(3): The proceeds of all taxes levied under this chapter are appropriated to this fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-108(4): The state treasurer may create separate accounts within the sinking fund for each series of bonds issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-109 Payment of interest, principal, and redemption premiums.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-109(1): The Division of Finance shall draw warrants on the state treasury before any interest, principal, or redemption premiums become due on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-109(2): After receipt of the warrants, the state treasurer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-109(2)(a): promptly pay the warrants from funds within the sinking fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-109(2)(b): immediately transmit the amount paid to the paying agent for the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-110 Investment of sinking fund money.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-110(1): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The state treasurer may, by following the procedures and requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-110(2): Unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter, the treasurer shall retain all income from the investment of any money contained in the sinking fund in the sinking fund and use it for the payment of debt service on the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111 Bond proceeds -- Deposits -- Investment -- Disposition of investment income and unexpended proceeds.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(1)(a): Proceeds from the sale of bonds issued under this chapter shall be deposited within one or more accounts as determined by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(1)(b): The state treasurer shall administer and maintain these accounts unless otherwise provided by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(1)(c): The commission by resolution may provide for the deposit of the money with a trustee and the administration, disposition, or investment of the money by this trustee.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(2)(a): The commission by resolution shall provide for the kinds of investments in which the proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter may be invested.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(2)(b): Income from the investment of proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be applied as provided by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-111(3): Any unexpended bond proceeds issued under this chapter shall be deposited, upon completion of the purposes for which the bonds were issued, in the sinking fund, unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-112 Refunding of bonds.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-112(1): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act The commission may provide for the refunding of any of the bonds in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-112(2): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act For purposes of


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-113 Certification of satisfaction of conditions precedent -- Conclusiveness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-113(1): The commission may not issue any bond under this chapter until it finds and certifies that all conditions precedent to issuance of the bonds have been satisfied.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-113(2): A recital on any bond of this finding and certification conclusively establishes the completion and satisfaction of all conditions precedent.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-114 Tax exemption.
----------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter, any interest paid on the bonds, and any income from the bonds are not taxable in this state for any purpose, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-115 Legal investment status.
--------------------------------------------------------
Bonds issued under this chapter are legal investments for all state trust funds, insurance companies, banks, trust companies, and the State School Fund and may be used as collateral to secure legal obligations.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116 Publication of resolution or notice -- Limitation on actions to contest legality.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(1): 45-1-101; 11-14-316(2) The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(1)(a): 45-1-101 publish any resolution it adopts under this chapter:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(1)(a)(i): once in a newspaper having general circulation in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(1)(a)(ii): 45-1-101 as required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(1)(b): 11-14-316(2) in lieu of publishing the entire resolution, publish a notice of bonds to be issued, titled as such, containing the information required in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(2)(a): Any interested person, for 30 days after the date of publication, may contest:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(2)(a)(i): the legality of the resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(2)(a)(ii): any of the bonds authorized under it; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(2)(a)(iii): any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-116(2)(b): After 30 days, a person may not contest the legality of the resolution, any of the bonds authorized under it, or any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds for any cause.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-117 Report to Legislature.
------------------------------------------------------
The governor shall report the commission's proceedings to each annual general session of the Legislature in his budget for as long as bonds issued under this chapter remain outstanding.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-205(6)(a): by resolution, provide for payment to the United States of whatever amounts are necessary to comply with Section 148 (f) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-205(6)(b): enter into agreements with financial and other institutions and attorneys to provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-205(6)(b)(i): the calculation, holding, and payment of those amounts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-205(6)(b)(ii): payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under any agreements entered into by the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-206 Constitutional debt limitation.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-206(1): The commission may not issue bonds under this chapter in an amount that violates the limitation described in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-206(2): For purposes of applying the debt limitation contained in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1, the value of the taxable property in Utah is considered to be 100% of the fair market value of the taxable property of the state, as computed from the last assessment for state purposes previous to the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207 Tax levy -- Abatement of tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(1): Each year after issuance of the bonds and until all outstanding bonds are retired, there is levied a direct annual tax on all real and personal property within the state subject to state taxation, sufficient to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(1)(a): applicable bond redemption premiums, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(1)(b): interest on the bonds as it becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(1)(c): principal of the bonds as it becomes due.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(2)(a): The State Tax Commission shall fix the rate of the direct annual tax levy each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(2)(b): The tax shall be collected and the proceeds applied as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-207(3): The direct annual tax imposed under this section is abated to the extent money is available from sources, other than ad valorem taxes in the sinking fund, for the payment of bond interest, principal, and redemption premiums.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-208 Creation of sinking fund.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-208(1): There is created a sinking fund, to be administered by the state treasurer, entitled the "1997 Highway General Obligation Bonds Sinking Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-208(2): All money deposited in the sinking fund, from whatever source, shall be used to pay debt service on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-208(3): The proceeds of all taxes levied under this chapter are appropriated to this fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-208(4): The state treasurer may create separate accounts within the sinking fund for each series of bonds issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-209 Payment of interest, principal, and redemption premiums.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-209(1): The Division of Finance shall draw warrants on the state treasury before any interest, principal, or redemption premiums become due on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-209(2): After receipt of the warrants, the state treasurer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-209(2)(a): promptly pay the warrants from funds within the sinking fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-209(2)(b): immediately transmit the amount paid to the paying agent for the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-210 Investment of sinking fund money.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-210(1): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The state treasurer may, by following the procedures and requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-210(2): Unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter, the treasurer shall retain all income from the investment of any money contained in the sinking fund in the sinking fund and use it for the payment of debt service on the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211 Bond proceeds -- Deposits -- Investment -- Disposition of investment income and unexpended proceeds.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(1)(a): Proceeds from the sale of bonds issued under this chapter shall be deposited within one or more accounts as determined by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(1)(b): The state treasurer shall administer and maintain these accounts unless otherwise provided by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(1)(c): The commission, by resolution, may provide for the deposit of the money with a trustee and the administration, disposition, or investment of the money by this trustee.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(2)(a): The commission, by resolution, shall provide for the kinds of investments in which the proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter may be invested.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(2)(b): Income from the investment of proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be applied as provided by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-211(3): Any unexpended bond proceeds issued under this chapter shall be deposited, upon completion of the purposes for which the bonds were issued, in the sinking fund, unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-212 Refunding of bonds.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-212(1): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act The commission may provide for the refunding of any of the bonds in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-212(2): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act For purposes of


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-213 Certification of satisfaction of conditions precedent -- Conclusiveness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-213(1): The commission may not issue any bond under this chapter until it finds and certifies that all conditions precedent to issuance of the bonds have been satisfied.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-213(2): A recital on any bond of this finding and certification conclusively establishes the completion and satisfaction of all such conditions.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-214 Tax exemption.
----------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter, any interest paid on the bonds, and any income from the bonds are not taxable in this state for any purpose, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-215 Legal investment status.
--------------------------------------------------------
Bonds issued under this chapter are legal investments for all state trust funds, insurance companies, banks, trust companies, and the State School Fund and may be used as collateral to secure legal obligations.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216 Publication of resolution or notice -- Limitation on actions to contest legality.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(1): 45-1-101; 11-14-316(2) The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(1)(a): 45-1-101 publish any resolution it adopts under this chapter:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(1)(a)(i): once in a newspaper having general circulation in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(1)(a)(ii): 45-1-101 as required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(1)(b): 11-14-316(2) in lieu of publishing the entire resolution, publish a notice of bonds to be issued, titled as such, containing the information required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(2)(a): Any interested person, for 30 days after the date of publication, may contest:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(2)(a)(i): the legality of the resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(2)(a)(ii): any of the bonds authorized under it; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(2)(a)(iii): any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-216(2)(b): After 30 days, a person may not contest the legality of the resolution, any of the bonds authorized under it, or any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds for any cause.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-217 Report to Legislature.
------------------------------------------------------
The governor shall report the commission's proceedings to each annual general session of the Legislature in his budget for as long as bonds issued under this chapter remain outstanding.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(1): Part 2, 1997 Highway General Obligation Bond Authorization "Bond anticipation note" means a note issued in anticipation of the receipt of the proceeds of the sale of the bonds authorized under
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(2): "Flexible note" means a bond anticipation note whose interest is payable at, and on one or more dates before, maturity.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3)(a): "Short-term series note" means a bond anticipation note that is one of a series of notes issued pursuant to a financing program under which it is expected that:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3)(a)(i): each note will be paid from the proceeds of one or more renewal notes of that series; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3)(a)(ii): the final note or notes of the series will be paid from:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3)(a)(ii)(A): the proceeds of bonds in anticipation of the receipt of which the note or notes were issued; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3)(a)(ii)(B): money of the state on hand and legally available for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-301(3)(b): "Short-term series note" includes any note issued pursuant to a revolving credit agreement or other similar liquidity facility for the purpose of renewing or paying outstanding short-term series notes on their stated maturity dates when those short-term series notes are not renewed or paid from the proceeds of one or more other renewal notes of the series.

---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-302(1): The state treasurer may, by written order, issue bond anticipation notes and renewals of bond anticipation notes, including, but not limited to, flexible notes and short-term series notes, in the form and with the terms that he determines.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-302(4)(d): (4)(a); (b); (c) any combination of Subsections

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-302(8): Part 2, 1997 Highway General Obligation Bond Authorization; (8)(b)(i); (ii) Each note and any renewal of any note, with the interest on the note or renewal, shall be:

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-404 Manner of issuance -- Amounts, interest, and maturity.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-404(1): Bonds issued under this chapter may be authorized, sold, and issued at times and in a manner determined by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-404(2): Bonds may be issued in one or more series, in amounts, and shall bear dates, interest rate or rates, including a variable rate, and maturity dates as the commission determines by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-404(3): A bond issued may not mature later than 20 years after the date of final passage of this chapter.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(3)(d): A facsimile of the state seal may be imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(4):

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(4)(b): Bonds in changed denominations shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(4)(b)(i): be exchanged for the original bonds in like aggregate principal amounts and in a manner that prevents the duplication of interest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(4)(b)(ii): bear interest at the same rate, mature on the same date, and be as nearly as practicable in the form of the original bonds.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(5)(b): The commission may provide for the services and payment for the services of one or more financial institutions or other entities or persons, or nominees, within or outside the state, for the authentication, registration, transfer, including record, bookkeeping, or book entry functions, exchange, and payment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-405(5)(c): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305 The records of ownership, registration, transfer, and exchange of the bonds, and of persons to whom payment with respect to the obligations are made, are private records as provided in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-406 Constitutional debt limitation.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-406(1): The commission may not issue bonds under this chapter in an amount that violates the limitation described in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-406(2): For purposes of applying the debt limitation contained in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1, the value of the taxable property in Utah is considered to be 100% of the fair market value of the taxable property of the state, as computed from the last assessment for state purposes previous to the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407 Tax levy -- Abatement of tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(1): Each year after issuance of the bonds and until all outstanding bonds are retired, there is levied a direct annual tax on all real and personal property within the state subject to state taxation, sufficient to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(1)(a): applicable bond redemption premiums, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(1)(b): interest on the bonds as it becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(1)(c): principal of the bonds as it becomes due.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(2)(a): The State Tax Commission shall fix the rate of the direct annual tax levy each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(2)(b): The tax shall be collected and the proceeds applied as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-407(3): The direct annual tax imposed under this section is abated to the extent money is available from sources, other than ad valorem taxes in the sinking fund, for the payment of bond interest, principal, and redemption premiums.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-408 Creation of sinking fund.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-408(1): There is created a sinking fund, to be administered by the state treasurer, entitled the "1997 General Obligation Project Bonds Sinking Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-408(2): All money deposited in the sinking fund, from whatever source, shall be used to pay debt service on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-408(3): The proceeds of all taxes levied under this chapter are appropriated to this fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-408(4): The state treasurer may create separate accounts within the sinking fund for each series of bonds issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-409 Payment of interest, principal, and redemption premiums.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-409(1): The Division of Finance shall draw warrants on the state treasury before any interest, principal, or redemption premiums become due on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-409(2): After receipt of the warrants, the state treasurer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-409(2)(a): promptly pay the warrants from funds within the sinking fund; and

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-410 Investment of sinking fund money.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411 Bond proceeds -- Deposits -- Investment -- Disposition of investment income and unexpended proceeds.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(1)(a): Proceeds from the sale of bonds issued under this chapter shall be deposited within one or more accounts as determined by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(1)(b): The state treasurer shall administer and maintain these accounts unless otherwise provided by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(1)(c): The commission by resolution may provide for the deposit of the money with a trustee and the administration, disposition, or investment of the money by this trustee.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(2)(a): The commission by resolution shall provide for the kinds of investments in which the proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter may be invested.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(2)(b): Income from the investment of proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be applied as provided by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-411(3): Any unexpended bond proceeds issued under this chapter shall be deposited, upon completion of the purposes for which the bonds were issued, in the sinking fund, unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-412 Refunding of bonds.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-412(1): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act The commission may provide for the refunding of any of the bonds in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-412(2): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act For purposes of


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-413 Certification of satisfaction of conditions precedent -- Conclusiveness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-413(1): The commission may not issue any bond under this chapter until it finds and certifies that all conditions precedent to issuance of the bonds have been satisfied.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-413(2): A recital on any bond of this finding and certification conclusively establishes the completion and satisfaction of all conditions precedent.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-414 Tax exemption.
----------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter, any interest paid on the bonds, and any income from the bonds are not taxable in this state for any purpose, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-415 Legal investment status.
--------------------------------------------------------
Bonds issued under this chapter are legal investments for all state trust funds, insurance companies, banks, trust companies, and the State School Fund and may be used as collateral to secure legal obligations.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416 Publication of resolution or notice -- Limitation on actions to contest legality.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(1): 45-1-101; 11-14-316(2) The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(1)(a): 45-1-101 publish any resolution it adopts under this chapter:

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(2)(a): Any interested person, for 30 days after the date of publication, may contest:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(2)(a)(i): the legality of the resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(2)(a)(ii): any of the bonds authorized under it; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(2)(a)(iii): any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-416(2)(b): After 30 days, a person may not contest the legality of the resolution, any of the bonds authorized under it, or any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds for any cause.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-6-417 Report to Legislature.
------------------------------------------------------
The governor shall report the commission's proceedings to each annual general session of the Legislature in his budget for as long as bonds issued under this chapter remain outstanding.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-104 Manner of issuance -- Amounts, interest, and maturity.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-104(1): Bonds issued under this chapter may be authorized, sold, and issued at times and in a manner determined by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-104(2): Bonds may be issued in one or more series, in amounts, and shall bear dates, interest rate or rates, including a variable rate, and maturity dates as the commission determines by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-104(3): A bond issued may not mature later than 20 years after the date of final passage of this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105 Terms and conditions of sale -- Plan of financing -- Signatures -- Replacement -- Registration -- Federal rebate.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1): In the issuance of bonds, the commission may determine by resolution:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(a): the manner of sale, including public or private sale;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(b): the terms and conditions of sale, including price, whether at, below, or above face value;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(c): denominations;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(d): form;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(e): manner of execution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(f): manner of authentication;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(g): place and medium of purchase;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(h): redemption terms; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(1)(i): other provisions and details it considers appropriate.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(2): The commission may by resolution adopt a plan of financing, which may include terms and conditions of arrangements entered into by the commission on behalf of the state with financial and other institutions for letters of credit, standby letters of credit, reimbursement agreements, and remarketing, indexing, and tender agent agreements to secure the bonds, including payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under the agreements entered into by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(3)(a): Any signature of a public official authorized by resolution of the commission to sign the bonds may be a facsimile signature of that official imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(3)(b): If all signatures of public officials on the bonds are facsimile signatures, provision shall be made for a manual authenticating signature on the bonds by or on behalf of a designated authentication agent.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(3)(c): If an official ceases to hold office before delivery of the bonds signed by that official, the signature or facsimile signature of the official is nevertheless valid for all purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(3)(d): A facsimile of the state seal may be imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(4)(a): The commission may enact resolutions providing for the replacement of lost, destroyed, or mutilated bonds, or for the exchange of bonds after issuance for bonds of smaller or larger denominations.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(4)(b): Bonds in changed denominations shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(4)(b)(i): be exchanged for the original bonds in like aggregate principal amounts and in a manner that prevents the duplication of interest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(4)(b)(ii): bear interest at the same rate, mature on the same date, and be as nearly as practicable in the form of the original bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(5): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305; Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(5)(a): Bonds may be registered as to both principal and interest or may be in a book entry form under which the right to principal and interest may be transferred only through a book entry.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(5)(b): The commission may provide for the services and payment for the services of one or more financial institutions or other entities or persons, or nominees, within or outside the state, for the authentication, registration, transfer, including record, bookkeeping, or book entry functions, exchange, and payment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(5)(c): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305 The records of ownership, registration, transfer, and exchange of the bonds, and of persons to whom payment with respect to the obligations are made, are private records as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(5)(d): Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act The bonds and any evidences of participation interest in the bonds may be issued, executed, authenticated, registered, transferred, exchanged, and otherwise made to comply with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(6): The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(6)(a): by resolution, provide for payment to the United States of whatever amounts are necessary to comply with Section 148 (f) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(6)(b): enter into agreements with financial and other institutions and attorneys to provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(6)(b)(i): the calculation, holding, and payment of those amounts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-105(6)(b)(ii): payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under any agreements entered into by the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-106 Constitutional debt limitation.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-106(1): The commission may not issue bonds under this chapter in an amount that violates the limitation described in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-106(2): For purposes of applying the debt limitation contained in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1, the value of the taxable property in Utah is considered to be 100% of the fair market value of the taxable property of the state, as computed from the last assessment for state purposes previous to the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107 Tax levy -- Abatement of tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(1): Each year after issuance of the bonds and until all outstanding bonds are retired, there is levied a direct annual tax on all real and personal property within the state subject to state taxation, sufficient to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(1)(a): applicable bond redemption premiums, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(1)(b): interest on the bonds as it becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(1)(c): principal of the bonds as it becomes due.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(2)(a): The State Tax Commission shall fix the rate of the direct annual tax levy each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(2)(b): The tax shall be collected and the proceeds applied as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-107(3): The direct annual tax imposed under this section is abated to the extent money is available from sources, other than ad valorem taxes in the sinking fund, for the payment of bond interest, principal, and redemption premiums.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-108 Creation of sinking fund.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-108(1): There is created a sinking fund, to be administered by the state treasurer, entitled the "1998 General Obligation Bonds Sinking Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-108(2): All money deposited in the sinking fund, from whatever source, shall be used to pay debt service on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-108(3): The proceeds of all taxes levied under this chapter are appropriated to this fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-108(4): The state treasurer may create separate accounts within the sinking fund for each series of bonds issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-109 Payment of interest, principal, and redemption premiums.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-109(1): The Division of Finance shall draw warrants on the state treasury before any interest, principal, or redemption premiums become due on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-109(2): After receipt of the warrants, the state treasurer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-109(2)(a): promptly pay the warrants from funds within the sinking fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-109(2)(b): immediately transmit the amount paid to the paying agent for the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-110 Investment of sinking fund money.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-110(1): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The state treasurer may, by following the procedures and requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-110(2): Unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter, the treasurer shall retain all income from the investment of any money contained in the sinking fund in the sinking fund and use it for the payment of debt service on the bonds.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-114 Tax exemption.
----------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter, any interest paid on the bonds, and any income from the bonds are not taxable in this state for any purpose, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-115 Legal investment status.

Bonds issued under this chapter are legal investments for all state trust funds, insurance companies, banks, trust companies, and the State School Fund and may be used as collateral to secure legal obligations.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-203 Bond proceeds may be used to pay costs of issuance and sale.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be used for the purposes described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-204 Manner of issuance -- Amounts, interest, and maturity.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-204(1): Bonds issued under this chapter may be authorized, sold, and issued at times and in a manner determined by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-204(2): Bonds may be issued in one or more series, in amounts, and shall bear dates, interest rates, including a variable rate, and maturity dates as the commission determines by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-204(3): A bond issued may not mature later than 15 years after the date of final passage of this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205 Terms and conditions of sale -- Plan of financing -- Signatures -- Replacement -- Registration -- Federal rebate.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1): In the issuance of bonds, the commission may determine by resolution:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(a): the manner of sale, including public or private sale;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(b): the terms and conditions of sale, including price, whether at, below, or above face value;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(c): denominations;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(d): form;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(e): manner of execution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(f): manner of authentication;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(g): place and medium of purchase;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(h): redemption terms; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(1)(i): other provisions and details it considers appropriate.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(2): The commission may, by resolution, adopt a plan of financing, which may include terms and conditions of arrangements entered into by the commission on behalf of the state with financial and other institutions for letters of credit, standby letters of credit, reimbursement agreements, and remarketing, indexing, and tender agent agreements to secure the bonds, including payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under the agreements entered into by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(3)(a): Any signature of a public official authorized by resolution of the commission to sign the bonds may be a facsimile signature of that official imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(3)(b): If all signatures of public officials on the bonds are facsimile signatures, provision shall be made for a manual authenticating signature on the bonds by or on behalf of a designated authentication agent.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(3)(c): If an official ceases to hold office before delivery of the bonds signed by that official, the signature or facsimile signature of the official is nevertheless valid for all purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(3)(d): A facsimile of the state seal may be imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(4)(a): The commission may enact resolutions providing for the replacement of lost, destroyed, or mutilated bonds, or for the exchange of bonds after issuance for bonds of smaller or larger denominations.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(4)(b): Bonds in changed denominations shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(4)(b)(i): be exchanged for the original bonds in like aggregate principal amounts and in a manner that prevents the duplication of interest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(4)(b)(ii): bear interest at the same rate, mature on the same date, and be as nearly as practicable in the form of the original bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(5): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305; Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(5)(a): Bonds may be registered as to both principal and interest or may be in a book entry form under which the right to principal and interest may be transferred only through a book entry.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(5)(b): The commission may provide for the services and payment for the services of one or more financial institutions or other entities or persons, or nominees, within or outside the state, for the authentication, registration, transfer, including record, bookkeeping, or book entry functions, exchange, and payment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(5)(c): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305 The records of ownership, registration, transfer, and exchange of the bonds, and of persons to whom payment with respect to the obligations is made, are private records as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(5)(d): Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act The bonds and any evidences of participation interest in the bonds may be issued, executed, authenticated, registered, transferred, exchanged, and otherwise made to comply with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(6): The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(6)(a): by resolution, provide for payment to the United States of whatever amounts are necessary to comply with Section 148 (f) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(6)(b): enter into agreements with financial and other institutions and attorneys to provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(6)(b)(i): the calculation, holding, and payment of those amounts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-205(6)(b)(ii): payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under any agreements entered into by the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-206 Constitutional debt limitation.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-206(1): The commission may not issue bonds under this chapter in an amount that violates the limitation described in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-206(2): For purposes of applying the debt limitation contained in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1, the value of the taxable property in Utah is considered to be 100% of the fair market value of the taxable property of the state, as computed from the last assessment for state purposes previous to the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207 Tax levy -- Abatement of tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(1): Each year after issuance of the bonds and until all outstanding bonds are retired, there is levied a direct annual tax on all real and personal property within the state subject to state taxation, sufficient to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(1)(a): applicable bond redemption premiums, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(1)(b): interest on the bonds as it becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(1)(c): principal of the bonds as it becomes due.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(2)(a): The State Tax Commission shall fix the rate of the direct annual tax levy each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(2)(b): The tax shall be collected and the proceeds applied as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-207(3): The direct annual tax imposed under this section is abated to the extent money is available from sources, other than ad valorem taxes in the sinking fund, for the payment of bond interest, principal, and redemption premiums.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-208 Creation of sinking fund.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-208(1): There is created a sinking fund, to be administered by the state treasurer, entitled the "1998 Highway General Obligation Bonds Sinking Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-208(2): All money deposited in the sinking fund, from whatever source, shall be used to pay debt service on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-208(3): The proceeds of all taxes levied under this chapter are appropriated to this fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-208(4): The state treasurer may create separate accounts within the sinking fund for each series of bonds issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-209 Payment of interest, principal, and redemption premiums.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-209(1): The Division of Finance shall draw warrants on the state treasury before any interest, principal, or redemption premiums become due on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-209(2): After receipt of the warrants, the state treasurer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-209(2)(a): promptly pay the warrants from funds within the sinking fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-209(2)(b): immediately transmit the amount paid to the paying agent for the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-210 Investment of sinking fund money.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-210(1): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The state treasurer may, by following the procedures and requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-210(2): Unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter, the treasurer shall retain all income from the investment of any money contained in the sinking fund in the sinking fund and use it for the payment of debt service on the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211 Bond proceeds -- Deposits -- Investment -- Disposition of investment income and unexpended proceeds.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(1)(a): Proceeds from the sale of bonds issued under this chapter shall be deposited within one or more accounts as determined by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(1)(b): The state treasurer shall administer and maintain these accounts unless otherwise provided by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(1)(c): The commission, by resolution, may provide for the deposit of the money with a trustee and the administration, disposition, or investment of the money by this trustee.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(2)(a): The commission, by resolution, shall provide for the kinds of investments in which the proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter may be invested.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(2)(b): Income from the investment of proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be applied as provided by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-211(3): Any unexpended bond proceeds issued under this chapter shall be deposited, upon completion of the purposes for which the bonds were issued, in the sinking fund, unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-212 Refunding of bonds.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-212(1): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act The commission may provide for the refunding of any of the bonds in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-212(2): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act For purposes of


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-213 Certification of satisfaction of conditions precedent -- Conclusiveness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-213(1): The commission may not issue any bond under this chapter until it finds and certifies that all conditions precedent to issuance of the bonds have been satisfied.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-213(2): A recital on any bond of this finding and certification conclusively establishes the completion and satisfaction of all such conditions.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-214 Tax exemption.
----------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter, any interest paid on the bonds, and any income from the bonds are not taxable in this state for any purpose, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-215 Legal investment status.
--------------------------------------------------------
Bonds issued under this chapter are legal investments for all state trust funds, insurance companies, banks, trust companies, and the State School Fund and may be used as collateral to secure legal obligations.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216 Publication of resolution or notice -- Limitation on actions to contest legality.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(1): 45-1-101; 11-14-316(2) The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(1)(a): 45-1-101 publish any resolution it adopts under this chapter:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(1)(a)(i): once in a newspaper having general circulation in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(1)(a)(ii): 45-1-101 as required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(1)(b): 11-14-316(2) in lieu of publishing the entire resolution, publish a notice of bonds to be issued, titled as such, containing the information required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(2)(a): Any interested person, for 30 days after the date of publication, may contest:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(2)(a)(i): the legality of the resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(2)(a)(ii): any of the bonds authorized under it; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(2)(a)(iii): any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-216(2)(b): After 30 days, a person may not contest the legality of the resolution, any of the bonds authorized under it, or any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds for any cause.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-217 Report to Legislature.
------------------------------------------------------
The governor shall report the commission's proceedings to each annual general session of the Legislature in his budget for as long as bonds issued under this chapter remain outstanding.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(1): Part 2, 1998 Highway General Obligation Bond Authorization "Bond anticipation note" means a note issued in anticipation of the receipt of the proceeds of the sale of the bonds authorized under
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(2): "Flexible note" means a bond anticipation note whose interest is payable at, and on one or more dates before, maturity.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3)(a): "Short-term series note" means a bond anticipation note that is one of a series of notes issued pursuant to a financing program under which it is expected that:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3)(a)(i): each note will be paid from the proceeds of one or more renewal notes of that series; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3)(a)(ii): the final note or notes of the series will be paid from:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3)(a)(ii)(A): the proceeds of bonds in anticipation of the receipt of which the note or notes were issued; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3)(a)(ii)(B): money of the state on hand and legally available for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-301(3)(b): "Short-term series note" includes any note issued pursuant to a revolving credit agreement or other similar liquidity facility for the purpose of renewing or paying outstanding short-term series notes on their stated maturity dates when those short-term series notes are not renewed or paid from the proceeds of one or more other renewal notes of the series.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(3)(d): A facsimile of the state seal may be imprinted, engraved, stamped, or otherwise placed on the bonds.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(4)(b): Bonds in changed denominations shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(4)(b)(i): be exchanged for the original bonds in like aggregate principal amounts and in a manner that prevents the duplication of interest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(4)(b)(ii): bear interest at the same rate, mature on the same date, and be as nearly as practicable in the form of the original bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(5): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305; Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(5)(a): Bonds may be registered as to both principal and interest or may be in a book entry form under which the right to principal and interest may be transferred only through a book entry.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(5)(b): The commission may provide for the services and payment for the services of one or more financial institutions or other entities or persons, or nominees, within or outside the state, for the authentication, registration, transfer, including record, bookkeeping, or book entry functions, exchange, and payment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(5)(c): 63G-2-302; 63G-2-305 The records of ownership, registration, transfer, and exchange of the bonds, and of persons to whom payment with respect to the obligations are made, are private records as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(5)(d): Title 15, Chapter 7, Registered Public Obligations Act The bonds and any evidences of participation interest in the bonds may be issued, executed, authenticated, registered, transferred, exchanged, and otherwise made to comply with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(6): The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(6)(a): by resolution, provide for payment to the United States of whatever amounts are necessary to comply with Section 148 (f) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(6)(b): enter into agreements with financial and other institutions and attorneys to provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(6)(b)(i): the calculation, holding, and payment of those amounts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-405(6)(b)(ii): payment from any legally available source of fees, charges, or other amounts coming due under any agreements entered into by the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-406 Constitutional debt limitation.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-406(1): The commission may not issue bonds under this chapter in an amount that violates the limitation described in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-406(2): For purposes of applying the debt limitation contained in Utah Constitution Article XIV, Section 1, the value of the taxable property in Utah is considered to be 100% of the fair market value of the taxable property of the state, as computed from the last assessment for state purposes previous to the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407 Tax levy -- Abatement of tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(1): Each year after issuance of the bonds and until all outstanding bonds are retired, there is levied a direct annual tax on all real and personal property within the state subject to state taxation, sufficient to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(1)(a): applicable bond redemption premiums, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(1)(b): interest on the bonds as it becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(1)(c): principal of the bonds as it becomes due.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(2)(a): The State Tax Commission shall fix the rate of the direct annual tax levy each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(2)(b): The tax shall be collected and the proceeds applied as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-407(3): The direct annual tax imposed under this section is abated to the extent money is available from sources, other than ad valorem taxes in the sinking fund, for the payment of bond interest, principal, and redemption premiums.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-408 Creation of sinking fund.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-408(1): There is created a sinking fund, to be administered by the state treasurer, entitled the "1998 General Obligation Project Bonds Sinking Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-408(2): All money deposited in the sinking fund, from whatever source, shall be used to pay debt service on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-408(3): The proceeds of all taxes levied under this chapter are appropriated to this fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-408(4): The state treasurer may create separate accounts within the sinking fund for each series of bonds issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-409 Payment of interest, principal, and redemption premiums.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-409(1): The Division of Finance shall draw warrants on the state treasury before any interest, principal, or redemption premiums become due on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-409(2): After receipt of the warrants, the state treasurer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-409(2)(a): promptly pay the warrants from funds within the sinking fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-409(2)(b): immediately transmit the amount paid to the paying agent for the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-410 Investment of sinking fund money.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-410(1): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The state treasurer may, by following the procedures and requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-410(2): Unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter, the treasurer shall retain all income from the investment of any money contained in the sinking fund in the sinking fund and use it for the payment of debt service on the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411 Bond proceeds -- Deposits -- Investment -- Disposition of investment income and unexpended proceeds.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(1)(a): Proceeds from the sale of bonds issued under this chapter shall be deposited within one or more accounts as determined by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(1)(b): The state treasurer shall administer and maintain these accounts unless otherwise provided by the commission by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(1)(c): The commission by resolution may provide for the deposit of the money with a trustee and the administration, disposition, or investment of the money by this trustee.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(2)(a): The commission by resolution shall provide for the kinds of investments in which the proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter may be invested.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(2)(b): Income from the investment of proceeds of bonds issued under this chapter shall be applied as provided by resolution of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-411(3): Any unexpended bond proceeds issued under this chapter shall be deposited, upon completion of the purposes for which the bonds were issued, in the sinking fund, unless otherwise provided in the resolution of the commission authorizing the issuance of bonds under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-412 Refunding of bonds.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-412(1): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act The commission may provide for the refunding of any of the bonds in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-412(2): Title 11, Chapter 27, Utah Refunding Bond Act For purposes of


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-413 Certification of satisfaction of conditions precedent -- Conclusiveness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-413(1): The commission may not issue any bond under this chapter until it finds and certifies that all conditions precedent to issuance of the bonds have been satisfied.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-413(2): A recital on any bond of this finding and certification conclusively establishes the completion and satisfaction of all conditions precedent.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-414 Tax exemption.
----------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter, any interest paid on the bonds, and any income from the bonds are not taxable in this state for any purpose, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-415 Legal investment status.
--------------------------------------------------------
Bonds issued under this chapter are legal investments for all state trust funds, insurance companies, banks, trust companies, and the State School Fund and may be used as collateral to secure legal obligations.

Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416 Publication of resolution or notice -- Limitation on actions to contest legality.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(1): 45-1-101; 11-14-316(2) The commission may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(1)(a): 45-1-101 publish any resolution it adopts under this chapter:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(1)(a)(i): once in a newspaper having general circulation in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(1)(a)(ii): 45-1-101 as required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(1)(b): 11-14-316(2) in lieu of publishing the entire resolution, publish a notice of bonds to be issued, titled as such, containing the information required in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(2)(a): Any interested person, for 30 days after the date of publication, may contest:
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(2)(a)(i): the legality of the resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(2)(a)(ii): any of the bonds authorized under it; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(2)(a)(iii): any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-416(2)(b): After 30 days, a person may not contest the legality of the resolution, any of the bonds authorized under it, or any of the provisions made for the security and repayment of the bonds for any cause.


Utah Code Annotated § 63B-7-417 Report to Legislature.
------------------------------------------------------
The governor shall report the commission's proceedings to each annual general session of the Legislature in his budget for as long as bonds issued under this chapter remain outstanding.
